\DoxyCodeLine{2033 \textcolor{comment}{/* Khronos platform-\/specific types and definitions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2034 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035 \textcolor{comment}{ * The master copy of khrplatform.h is maintained in the Khronos EGL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036 \textcolor{comment}{ * Registry repository at https://github.com/KhronosGroup/EGL-\/Registry}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037 \textcolor{comment}{ * The last semantic modification to khrplatform.h was at commit ID:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038 \textcolor{comment}{ *      67a3e0864c2d75ea5287b9f3d2eb74a745936692}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040 \textcolor{comment}{ * Adopters may modify this file to suit their platform. Adopters are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041 \textcolor{comment}{ * encouraged to submit platform specific modifications to the Khronos}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2042 \textcolor{comment}{ * group so that they can be included in future versions of this file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043 \textcolor{comment}{ * Please submit changes by filing pull requests or issues on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044 \textcolor{comment}{ * the EGL Registry repository linked above.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047 \textcolor{comment}{ * See the Implementer's Guidelines for information about where this file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048 \textcolor{comment}{ * should be located on your system and for more details of its use:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2049 \textcolor{comment}{ *    http://www.khronos.org/registry/implementers\_guide.pdf}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051 \textcolor{comment}{ * This file should be included as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2052 \textcolor{comment}{ *        \#include <KHR/khrplatform.h>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2053 \textcolor{comment}{ * by Khronos client API header files that use its types and defines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2054 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2055 \textcolor{comment}{ * The types in khrplatform.h should only be used to define API-\/specific types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2056 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2057 \textcolor{comment}{ * Types defined in khrplatform.h:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2058 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int8\_t              signed   8  bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2059 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint8\_t             unsigned 8  bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2060 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int16\_t             signed   16 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2061 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint16\_t            unsigned 16 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2062 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int32\_t             signed   32 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2063 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint32\_t            unsigned 32 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2064 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int64\_t             signed   64 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2065 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint64\_t            unsigned 64 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2066 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_intptr\_t            signed   same number of bits as a pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2067 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uintptr\_t           unsigned same number of bits as a pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2068 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_ssize\_t             signed   size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_usize\_t             unsigned size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_float\_t             signed   32 bit floating point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_time\_ns\_t           unsigned 64 bit time in nanoseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_utime\_nanoseconds\_t unsigned time interval or absolute time in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2073 \textcolor{comment}{ *                                         nanoseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2074 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_stime\_nanoseconds\_t signed time interval in nanoseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_boolean\_enum\_t      enumerated boolean type. This should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076 \textcolor{comment}{ *      only be used as a base type when a client API's boolean type is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2077 \textcolor{comment}{ *      an enum. Client APIs which use an integer or other type for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2078 \textcolor{comment}{ *      booleans cannot use this as the base type for their boolean.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2079 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080 \textcolor{comment}{ * Tokens defined in khrplatform.h:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2081 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2082 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_FALSE, KHRONOS\_TRUE Enumerated boolean false/true values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2083 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2084 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_SUPPORT\_INT64 is 1 if 64 bit integers are supported; otherwise 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2085 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_SUPPORT\_FLOAT is 1 if floats are supported; otherwise 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2086 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2087 \textcolor{comment}{ * Calling convention macros defined in this file:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2088 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_APICALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2089 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_GLAD\_API\_PTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2090 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_APIATTRIBUTES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2091 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2092 \textcolor{comment}{ * These may be used in function prototypes as:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2093 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2094 \textcolor{comment}{ *      KHRONOS\_APICALL void KHRONOS\_GLAD\_API\_PTR funcname(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2095 \textcolor{comment}{ *                                  int arg1,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2096 \textcolor{comment}{ *                                  int arg2) KHRONOS\_APIATTRIBUTES;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2097 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2098 }

\DoxyCodeLine{8490 }
\DoxyCodeLine{8491 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glad\_gl\_find\_core\_gl(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{8492     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{8493     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* version;}
\DoxyCodeLine{8494     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* prefixes[] = \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{8495         \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}OpenGL ES-\/CM "{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{8496         \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}OpenGL ES-\/CL "{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{8497         \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}OpenGL ES "{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{8498         \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}OpenGL SC "{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{8499         NULL}
\DoxyCodeLine{8500     \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{8501     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} major = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{8502     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} minor = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{8503     version = (\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*) glad\_glGetString(GL\_VERSION);}
\DoxyCodeLine{8504     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!version) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{8505     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0;  prefixes[i];  i++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{8506         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} length = strlen(prefixes[i]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{8507         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (strncmp(version, prefixes[i], length) == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{8508             version += length;}
\DoxyCodeLine{8509             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
